# <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-12"></a><span data-ttu-id="8ab8c-103">Новые возможности API JavaScript для Excel 1.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8ab8c-103">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8ab8c-104">ExcelApi 1,2 добавлена поддержка фильтрации таблиц и доступа к встроенным функциям Excel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8ab8c-104">ExcelApi 1.2 added support for table filtering and access to built-in Excel functions.</span></span>
